Source Code

This is a reconstructed version of Luminary 130, the initial AGC program released in November 1969 for the Apollo 13 LM. Three more releases followed before the flown revision was finally manufactured in February 1970.

This reconstruction was created from a previous transcription of the original listing of Luminary 131, combined with Luminary memo #129 which describes the small difference between the Luminary 130 and 131. The reconstructed source code was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed for Luminary 130 in drawing 2021152G.

In this source code, program comments from the original (Luminary 131) code are prefixed with '#', while those added later by the Virtual AGC project are prefixed with '##'. 

016470,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016471,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016472,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of the reconstructed source code for Luminary 130.
016473,000005:                                                                                                  ##              This was the original program released for the Apollo 13 LM,
016474,000006:                                                                                                  ##              although several more revisions would follow. It has been
016475,000007:                                                                                                  ##              reconstructed from a listing of Luminary 131, from which it
016476,000008:                                                                                                  ##              differs on only two lines in P70-P71. The difference is
016477,000009:                                                                                                  ##              described in detail in Luminary memo #129, which was used
016478,000010:                                                                                                  ##              to perform the reconstruction. This file is intended to be a
016479,000011:                                                                                                  ##              faithful reconstruction, except that the code format has been
016480,000012:                                                                                                  ##              changed to conform to the requirements of the yaYUL assembler
016481,000013:                                                                                                  ##              rather than the original YUL assembler.
016482,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 392-475
016483,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016484,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo
016485,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/11/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
016486,000018:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/03 RSB.   First draft completed.
016487,000019:                                                                                                  ##              06/06/03 RSB.   Fixed a bunch of typos in the comments.

016491,000023:                                                                                                  ##                              numbers in 1701.pdf.

016509,000041:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016510,000042:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016511,000043:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016512,000044:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016513,000045: 
016514,000046:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016515,000047: 
016516,000048:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016517,000049:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016518,000050:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016519,000051:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016520,000052: 
016521,000053:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016522,000054:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016523,000055:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016524,000056:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016525,000057:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016526,000058: 
016527,000059:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016528,000060:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016529,000061:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016530,000062:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016531,000063: 
016532,000064:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016533,000065:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016534,000066: 
016535,000067:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016536,000068: 
016537,000069:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016538,000070:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016539,000071:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016540,000072:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016541,000073:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016542,000074: 
016543,000075:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016544,000076:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016545,000077:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016546,000078:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016547,000079: 
016548,000080:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016549,000081:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016550,000082:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016551,000083:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016552,000084:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016553,000085: 
016554,000086:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016555,000087: 
016556,000088:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016557,000089:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016558,000090:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 393 

016560,000092:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016561,000093:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016562,000094:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016563,000095:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016564,000096:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016565,000097:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016566,000098:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016567,000099:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016568,000100:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016569,000101:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016570,000102: 
016571,000103:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016572,000104:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016573,000105:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016574,000106: 
016575,000107:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016576,000108: 
016577,000109:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016578,000110:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016579,000111:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016580,000112: 
016581,000113:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016582,000114:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016583,000115:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016584,000116:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016585,000117:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016586,000118:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016587,000119:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016588,000120: 
016589,000121:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016590,000122:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016591,000123: 
016592,000124:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016593,000125: 
016594,000126:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016595,000127:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016596,000128:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016597,000129:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016598,000130: 
016599,000131:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016600,000132: 
016601,000133:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016602,000134:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016603,000135:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016604,000136:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016605,000137: 
016606,000138:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 394 

016608,000140:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016609,000141: 
016610,000142:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016611,000143: 
016612,000144:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016613,000145:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016614,000146: 
016615,000147:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016616,000148:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016617,000149:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016618,000150:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016619,000151: 
016620,000152:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016621,000153:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016622,000154: 
016623,000155:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016624,000156:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016625,000157:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016626,000158:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016627,000159: 
016628,000160:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016629,000161:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016630,000162: 
016631,000163:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016632,000164:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
016633,000165: 
016634,000166:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016635,000167: 
016636,000168:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016637,000169:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016638,000170:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016639,000171:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016640,000172: 
016641,000173:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016642,000174:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016643,000175: 
016644,000176:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016645,000177:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016646,000178: 
016647,000179:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016648,000180:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016649,000181:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016650,000182: 
016651,000183:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016652,000184: 
016653,000185:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016654,000186:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 395 

016656,000188:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016657,000189:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016658,000190: 
016659,000191:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016660,000192: 
016661,000193: 
016662,000194:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016663,000195: 
016664,000196:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016665,000197:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016666,000198:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
016667,000199:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016668,000200:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016669,000201:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016670,000202:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016671,000203:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016672,000204:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016673,000205:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016674,000206:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016675,000207:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016676,000208:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016677,000209:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016678,000210:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
016679,000211:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016680,000212:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016681,000213:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016682,000214:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016683,000215:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016684,000216:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016685,000217:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016686,000218:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
016687,000219:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016688,000220:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
016689,000221:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016690,000222:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016691,000223:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016692,000224:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016693,000225:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016694,000226:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016695,000227:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016696,000228:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016697,000229:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016698,000230:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016699,000231: 
016700,000232:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016701,000233:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

016724,000256:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)

016735,000267:

016761,000293:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
016762,000294:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016763,000295:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016764,000296:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016765,000297:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016766,000298:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016767,000299:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016768,000300:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016769,000301:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016770,000302:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016771,000303:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016772,000304: 
016773,000305:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016774,000306: 
016775,000307:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016776,000308: 
016777,000309:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016778,000310:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016779,000311:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016780,000312:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016781,000313:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016782,000314: 
016783,000315:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016784,000316: 
016785,000317:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016786,000318: 
016787,000319:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016788,000320:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016789,000321:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016790,000322: 
016791,000323:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016792,000324: 
016793,000325:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016794,000326: 
016795,000327:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016796,000328:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
016797,000329:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016798,000330: 
016799,000331:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016800,000332:

Page 398 

016802,000334:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016803,000335:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
016804,000336:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
016805,000337:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
016806,000338:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
016807,000339:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
016808,000340:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
016809,000341:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
016810,000342:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
016811,000343:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
016812,000344:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
016813,000345:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
016814,000346: 
016815,000347:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016816,000348:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016817,000349:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016818,000350:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016819,000351:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016820,000352:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016821,000353: 
016822,000354:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016823,000355:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
016824,000356:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
016825,000357:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
016826,000358:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
016827,000359:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
016828,000360: 
016829,000361:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016830,000362: 
016831,000363:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016832,000364:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
016833,000365:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
016834,000366:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
016835,000367:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
016836,000368:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
016837,000369:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
016838,000370:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
016839,000371:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
016840,000372:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
016841,000373:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
016842,000374: 
016843,000375:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016844,000376: 
016845,000377:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016846,000378:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
016847,000379:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016848,000380:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016849,000381:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016850,000382:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 399 

016852,000384:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016853,000385:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016854,000386:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016855,000387:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016856,000388:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016857,000389:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016858,000390:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016859,000391:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
016860,000392: 
016861,000393:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016862,000394: 
016863,000395:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
016864,000396:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
016865,000397:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
016866,000398:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
016867,000399:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
016868,000400:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
016869,000401:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
016870,000402:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
016871,000403:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
016872,000404:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
016873,000405:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
016874,000406: 
016875,000407:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016876,000408: 
016877,000409:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016878,000410:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016879,000411:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016880,000412:

017279,000811:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER

Page 415 

017571,001103:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017572,001104: 
017573,001105:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017574,001106:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
017575,001107:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017576,001108:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017577,001109:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017578,001110: 
017579,001111:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017580,001112:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017581,001113: 
017582,001114:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017583,001115: 
017584,001116:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017585,001117:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017586,001118:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017587,001119: 
017588,001120:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017589,001121:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017590,001122:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017591,001123:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017592,001124:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017593,001125:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017594,001126: 
017595,001127:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017596,001128:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017597,001129:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017598,001130:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017599,001131:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017600,001132: 
017601,001133:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017602,001134:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017603,001135: 
017604,001136:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017605,001137: 
017606,001138:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017607,001139:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017608,001140:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017609,001141:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017610,001142:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017611,001143: 
017612,001144:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017613,001145:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017614,001146:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017615,001147: 
017616,001148:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017617,001149:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017618,001150: 
017619,001151:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017620,001152:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
017621,001153:

Page 416 

017623,001155:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017624,001156:

018172,001704:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
018173,001705:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018174,001706:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018175,001707:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018176,001708:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018177,001709:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

018797,002329: 42,3605           04145                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
018798,002330: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
018799,002331:

Page 441 

018801,002333:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018802,002334:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018803,002335:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018804,002336:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018805,002337:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018806,002338: 
018807,002339:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018808,002340:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018809,002341:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
018810,002342:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
018811,002343:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018812,002344:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018813,002345:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018814,002346: 
018815,002347:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018816,002348:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018817,002349:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018818,002350: 
018819,002351:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018820,002352:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018821,002353: 
018822,002354:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE

018951,002483:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018952,002484:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
018953,002485:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018954,002486:                                                                                                  #  
018955,002487:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018956,002488: 
018957,002489:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018958,002490:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018959,002491:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018960,002492: 
018961,002493:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018962,002494:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018963,002495:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018964,002496: 
018965,002497: 41,3400           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018966,002498: 41,3401           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018967,002499: 41,3402           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018968,002500: 41,3403           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018969,002501: 41,3404           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018970,002502: 41,3405           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018971,002503: 41,3406           03410                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018972,002504: 41,3407           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019381,002913:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 454 

019383,002915: 
019384,002916:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019385,002917: 
019386,002918:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019387,002919: 
019388,002920:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019389,002921:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019390,002922:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019391,002923:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019392,002924: 
019393,002925:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019394,002926:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019395,002927:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019396,002928: 
019397,002929:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019398,002930:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019399,002931:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019400,002932:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019401,002933:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019402,002934:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019403,002935:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019404,002936:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019405,002937:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019406,002938:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019407,002939:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019408,002940: 
019409,002941: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019410,002942: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019411,002943: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019412,002944: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019413,002945: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019414,002946: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019415,002947: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019416,002948: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019417,002949: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019418,002950: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019419,002951: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019420,002952: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019421,002953: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019422,002954: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019423,002955: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019424,002956: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019425,002957: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019426,002958: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019427,002959: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019428,002960: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019429,002961: 
019430,002962: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019431,002963:

Page 455 

019433,002965:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
019434,002966:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019435,002967:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019436,002968:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019437,002969:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019438,002970: 
019439,002971:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019440,002972:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019441,002973:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019442,002974: 
019443,002975:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019444,002976:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019445,002977: 
019446,002978:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019447,002979:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019448,002980:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019449,002981:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019450,002982:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019451,002983: 
019452,002984:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019453,002985:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019454,002986:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019455,002987:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019456,002988: 
019457,002989:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019458,002990:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019459,002991:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019460,002992:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019461,002993:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019462,002994:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019463,002995:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019464,002996: 
019465,002997:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019466,002998:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019467,002999: 
019468,003000:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019469,003001:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019470,003002: 
019471,003003:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019472,003004:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019473,003005: 
019474,003006:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019475,003007:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019476,003008:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019477,003009:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019478,003010:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019479,003011:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019480,003012:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019481,003013: 
019482,003014:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 456 

019484,003016:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019485,003017:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019486,003018:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019487,003019:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019488,003020:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
019489,003021:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019490,003022:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019491,003023:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019492,003024:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019493,003025: 
019494,003026:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019495,003027:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019496,003028: 
019497,003029:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019498,003030: 
019499,003031:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019500,003032:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019501,003033:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019502,003034:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019503,003035:    4157           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019504,003036:    4160           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019505,003037:    4161           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019506,003038:    4162           00002                           TC       Q                                     #  DSP SYST BLOCKED.  RET TO 1+ CALLING LOC
019507,003039:    4163           34753                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
019508,003040:    4164           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
019509,003041:    4165           55036                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
019510,003042:    4166           23021                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019511,003043:    4167           04204                           TC       KILMONON                              #  TURN ON KILL MONITOR BIT

019528,003060:    4203           05165                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
019529,003061:
