019604,003136:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019605,003137: 
019606,003138:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019607,003139:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019608,003140:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019609,003141:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019610,003142:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019611,003143:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019612,003144:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019613,003145: 
019614,003146:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
019615,003147:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019616,003148:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019617,003149:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019618,003150:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
019619,003151: 
019620,003152:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019621,003153:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019622,003154:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019623,003155:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019624,003156:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019625,003157:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019626,003158:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019627,003159:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019628,003160:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019629,003161:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019630,003162: 
019631,003163:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 459 

019633,003165:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019634,003166:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019635,003167:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019636,003168:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019637,003169:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
019638,003170: 
019639,003171:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019640,003172:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019641,003173:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019642,003174:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019643,003175:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019644,003176:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019645,003177:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019646,003178:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019647,003179: 
019648,003180:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB

019691,003223: 
019692,003224:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019693,003225:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
019694,003226:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.

019696,003228:

019976,003508:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019977,003509: 
019978,003510:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019979,003511:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019980,003512:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019981,003513:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019982,003514: 
019983,003515:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019984,003516:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
019985,003517:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
019986,003518:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019987,003519:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019988,003520:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019989,003521:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019990,003522: 
019991,003523:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019992,003524:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019993,003525:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019994,003526:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019995,003527:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019996,003528: 
019997,003529:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019998,003530:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019999,003531:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020000,003532:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020001,003533:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020002,003534: 
020003,003535:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020004,003536:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
020005,003537:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
020006,003538: 
020007,003539: 
020008,003540:                                                                                                  #  .
020009,003541: 
020010,003542: 
020011,003543:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020012,003544:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020013,003545:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
020014,003546:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020015,003547: 
020016,003548:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020017,003549:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020018,003550:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020019,003551: 
020020,003552:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020021,003553:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
020022,003554:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 468 

020024,003556:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020025,003557: 
020026,003558:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020027,003559:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
020028,003560:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020029,003561:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
020030,003562:    4443           10633                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
020031,003563:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
020032,003564: 
020033,003565:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
020034,003566:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
020035,003567: 
020036,003568: 04,2633                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
020037,003569: 04,2633                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020038,003570: 04,2633           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
020039,003571: 04,2634           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020040,003572: 04,2635           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
020041,003573: 04,2636           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
020042,003574: 04,2637           30001                           CA       L                                     
020043,003575: 04,2640           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
020044,003576: 04,2641           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020045,003577: 
020046,003578:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
020047,003579:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
020048,003580:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
020049,003581:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
020050,003582:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
020051,003583: 
020052,003584:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
020053,003585:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020054,003586:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020055,003587:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
020056,003588:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020057,003589:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020058,003590:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
020059,003591:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020060,003592:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
020061,003593:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
020062,003594:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
020063,003595:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
020064,003596:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
020065,003597: 
020066,003598:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
020067,003599:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
020068,003600: 
020069,003601:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
020070,003602:

020220,003752:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020221,003753:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020222,003754:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020223,003755: 
020224,003756:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020225,003757:                                                                                                  #  
020226,003758:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020227,003759:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020228,003760:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
